                                   focusScroll3.circularly = true;
                                   focusScroll3.initialize(); //初始化

                                   SHM.dom.byId('SI_Scroll_eduopen_Arr_L').onmousedown = function(){
                                       focusScroll3.pre();
                                       return false;
                                   }

                                       focusScroll3.next();
